- ‚ö†Ô∏è Delete template ‚Üí no longer appears in import wizard
- ‚ö†Ô∏è Edit template column mappings ‚Üí changes reflected when used
- ‚ö†Ô∏è Platform templates read-only for org admins (can only clone)

**Status:** PARTIAL - Code is fully integrated and compiles, but end-to-end functional testing requires running app and manual verification.

**NONE** - All components properly imported and wired.

## Data Flow Verification

### Backend ‚Üí Frontend

**Templates List:**
1. ‚úÖ Query: `importTemplates.listTemplates` (backend: line 246)
2. ‚úÖ Called from: Templates page (lines 392-400) and Import wizard (page.tsx:266,272)
3. ‚úÖ Returns: Array of template objects with all fields
4. ‚úÖ Loading state: Checked with `!allTemplates` (line 445)
5. ‚úÖ Empty state: Checked with `filteredTemplates.length === 0` (line 577)

**Usage Stats:**
1. ‚úÖ Query: `importSessions.getTemplateUsageStats` (backend: line 278)
2. ‚úÖ Called from: Templates page (lines 415-418) with skip when no templates
3. ‚úÖ Uses index: `by_templateId` on importSessions table
4. ‚úÖ Data rendered: Via `usageMap` (lines 421-435), displayed in table (line 206) and cards (line 315)

**Mutations:**
1. ‚úÖ createTemplate: Wired to form submit (line 457), passes all form data (lines 458-469)
2. ‚úÖ updateTemplate: Wired to form submit (line 487), passes templateId + changes (lines 488-498)
3. ‚úÖ deleteTemplate: Wired to delete dialog (line 38 of delete-dialog.tsx)
4. ‚úÖ cloneTemplate: Wired to clone dialog (line 49 of clone-dialog.tsx), forces org scope for platform templates

## Common "Looks Done But Isn't" Issues - Status

1. ‚úÖ **Component exists but not imported** - All components imported and rendered
2. ‚úÖ **Query exists but no index** - `by_templateId` index exists in schema
3. ‚úÖ **Mutation exists but no UI calls it** - All mutations called from UI
4. ‚úÖ **Loading state missing** - Loading state checked (line 568)
5. ‚úÖ **Empty state missing** - Empty state shown (lines 577-589)
6. ‚úÖ **Navigation not wired** - Sidebar link exists and points to correct route
7. ‚úÖ **Authorization not checked** - Handled by parent layout (admin/layout.tsx)
8. ‚úÖ **Schema field added but not in query return** - Return validators include all fields

---

## Project-Specific Pattern Compliance

**Multi-tenancy:**
- ‚úÖ All queries filter by organizationId: listTemplates accepts scope + organizationId
- ‚úÖ Mutations verify permissions: Platform staff can create platform templates, org admins only org templates (line 399-426 in template-form.tsx)

**Convex patterns:**
- ‚úÖ `.withIndex()` not `.filter()`: getTemplateUsageStats uses index (line 294)
- ‚úÖ Returns validator: All queries/mutations have returns validator
- ‚úÖ Args validator: All queries/mutations have args validator

**Frontend patterns:**
- ‚úÖ `useQuery` result checked for undefined: Line 445 checks `!allTemplates`
- ‚úÖ `useQuery` uses "skip": Line 417 uses skip when `templateIds.length === 0`
- ‚úÖ No `useQuery` inside list item components: Queries lifted to parent, stats passed as props

**Better Auth:**
- ‚úÖ Uses `user._id`: Line 385, `const userId = user?._id ?? ""`
- ‚ö†Ô∏è Uses `user.name`: Not used in this phase (no user name display needed)

---

## Recommended Next Steps

1. **Run ultracite fix:**
   ```bash
   npx ultracite fix
   ```

2. **Manual functional testing (when dev server available):**
   - Create a template manually ‚Üí verify it appears in import wizard
   - Upload a sample CSV ‚Üí verify auto-mapping works ‚Üí save template ‚Üí use in import
   - Clone a platform template ‚Üí edit the clone ‚Üí use in import
   - Delete a template ‚Üí verify it no longer appears in import wizard
   - Edit template mappings ‚Üí verify changes reflected when template used

3. **Visual testing at 3 viewports:**
   - Desktop (1920x1080)
   - Tablet (768x812)
   - Mobile (375px minimum)

4. **Edge case testing:**
   - Empty templates list (no platform, no org templates)
   - Template with no sport specified
   - Template with many column mappings (scroll behavior)
   - Very long template names/descriptions (truncation)
